expressed themselves on Blogger. margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">Posts</span></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.38; Starting in late June, many Blogger creators will see the new interface become their default, though they can revert to the old interface by clicking ‚ÄúRevert to legacy Blogger‚Äù in the left-hand navigation. By late July, creators will no longer be able to revert to the legacy Blogger interface.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div><br /><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;"><span style="font-family: arial; font-size: 11pt; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;">We recommend getting ahead of the transition by opting into the experience today. <script type="text/javascript">
setREVStartSize({c: 'rev_slider_1_1',rl:[1240,1024,778,480],el:[750,600,600,500],gw:[1300,1100,600,300],gh:[750,600,600,500],type:'standard',justify:'',layout:'fullscreen',offsetContainer:'',offset:'',mh:"0"});
var	revapi1,
tpj;
function revinit_revslider11() {
jQuery(function() {
tpj = jQuery;
revapi1 = tpj("#rev_slider_1_1");
if(revapi1==undefined || revapi1.revolution == undefined){
revslider_showDoubleJqueryError("rev_slider_1_1");
}else{
revapi1.revolution({
DPR:"dpr",
sliderLayout:"fullscreen",
duration:4000,
visibilityLevels:"1240,1024,778,480",
gridwidth:"1300,1100,600,300",
gridheight:"750,600,600,500",
spinner:"spinner1",
perspective:600,
perspectiveType:"local",
editorheight:"750,600,600,500",
responsiveLevels:"1240,1024,778,480",
progressBar:{disableProgressBar:true},
navigation: {
mouseScrollNavigation:false,
wheelCallDelay:1000,
onHoverStop:false,
arrows: {
enable:true,
tmp:"<span class=\"edgtf-nav-arrow\"></span>",
style:"edge-light",
hide_onmobile:true,
hide_under:1025,
left: {
h_offset:5
},
right: {
h_offset:5
}
},
bullets: {
enable:true,
tmp:"",
style:"edge-light",
hide_over:1024,
v_offset:50,
space:20
}
},
parallax: {
levels:[5,10,15,20,25,30,35,40,45,46,47,48,49,50,51,55],
type:"mouse"
},
fanim: {
in:{"o":0},
out:{"a":false},
speed:300
},
viewPort: {
enable:true,
visible_area:"1%"
},
fallbacks: {
allowHTML5AutoPlayOnAndroid:true
},
});
}

});
} // End of RevInitScript
var once_revslider11 = false;
if (document.readyState === "loading") {document.addEventListener('readystatechange',function() { if((document.readyState === "interactive" || document.readyState === "complete") && !once_revslider11 ) { once_revslider11 = true; revinit_revslider11();}});} else {once_revslider11 = true; revinit_revslider11();}
</script>
<script>
var htmlDivCss = unescape("%23rev_slider_1_1_wrapper%20rs-loader.spinner1%7B%20background-color%3A%20%23FFFFFF%20%21important%3B%20%7D");
var htmlDiv = document.getElementById('rs-plugin-settings-inline-css');

htmlDiv.innerHTML = htmlDiv.innerHTML + htmlDivCss;
}else{

}

<div class="edgtf-section-title-holder  ">
<div class="edgtf-st-inner">
<h1 class="edgtf-st-title">
A cozy atmosphere<span class="edgtf-st-title-dot">.</span>			</h1>
<p class="edgtf-st-text" style="color: white; margin-top: 23px;">
Papa Legba‚Äôs mission is to provide a great place to relax and unwind, combining an intriguing atmosphere with excellent mixologist designed signature cocktails. The mission is not only to have a longstanding establishment contributing toward the enhancement of St.Paul‚Äôs west side neighborhood, it is also to offer guest a unique experience in an establishment where guest experience and satisfaction is paramount.			</p>
</div>

    <span class="edgtf-btn-text">Read More</span>

<div class="edgtf-section-title-holder">
<div class="edgtf-st-inner">
<h1 class="edgtf-st-title">
A cozy atmosphere<span class="edgtf-st-title-dot">.</span>			</h1>
<p class="edgtf-st-text" style="color: white; margin-top: 23px;">
Papa Legba‚Äôs mission is to provide a great place to relax and unwind, combining an intriguing atmosphere with excellent mixologist designed signature cocktails. The mission is not only to have a longstanding establishment contributing toward the enhancement of St.Paul‚Äôs west side neighborhood, it is also to offer guest a unique experience in an establishment where guest experience and satisfaction is paramount.			</p>
</div>
</div><div class="vc_empty_space" style="height: 61px;"><span class="vc_empty_space_inner"></span></div><a class="edgtf-btn edgtf-btn-medium edgtf-btn-outline edgtf-btn-orange-black edgtf-btn-custom-hover-bg edgtf-btn-custom-border-hover edgtf-btn-custom-hover-color" data-hover-bg-color="#ffffff" data-hover-border-color="#ffffff" data-hover-color="#000000" href="https://papalegbalounge.com/about/" itemprop="url" style="border-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: white;" target="_self">
    <span class="edgtf-btn-text">Read More</span>
